charged to an operating expense and then re-allocated to a capital asset FRA.</p><p>1) To record the purchase and receipt of the vehicle on January 31, 2000.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Vehicle</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23,500</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16133</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B14A(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1261</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Vehicle</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>500</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16133</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B14A(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>0210</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR GST Refundable Advance</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1,680</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>13392</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>G111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8171</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accounts payable</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,680</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale: </strong>The Department must capitalize this asset as a debit to the capital asset (vehicle) 
account, since it is above the $10,000 threshold. Delivery costs should be capitalized as part of the laid down cost of 
the asset. At this point the Department is being charged GST on the vehicle, and must pay it to the vendor. However, as 
the Department will eventually recover this amount from Canada Customs and Revenue Agency (CCRA), they should record it 
as an asset in "13392 GST/HST Refundable advance accounts". Since the Department has not paid for the vehicle, a liability 
must be recorded for the amount owing.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> (*) In this example it is assumed this purchase would be charged to the 
capital vote. However, depending on the department and the asset purchased, the following authority codes could be used: 
B11A - Program Vote, B12A Operating Vote, or A131 Spending of amounts equivalent to proceeds from disposal of surplus Crown 
assets. Since GST is not to be charged to a departmental appropriation, it is set up as an advance under a special authority, 
G111. There is no impact on authorities for the accounts payable so the code to be used would be "R300-All other assets 
and liabilities"</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> As economic objects are recorded on an expenditure basis, the economic object 
is recorded at this point. Economic object 1261 is used in this example since the purchase was a motor vehicle. The appropriate 
economic object is used depending on the nature of the purchase. Economic object "0210-Transportation of things not elsewhere 
specified" would be used to record freight. However, where a department's system cannot handle the use of more than one 
economic object for an asset, the cost of freight may be coded to the same object code as the asset. Since there is GST/HST 
payable, the GST must be reflected by using, "8171-Payment of GST on purchases". "6299-Net Increase or Decrease to Other 
Liability Accounts" is used to establish the accrual of the amount owing.</p><p><strong>Alternative set of entries:</strong> Departments may choose to record the purchase as an operating expense and 
reallocate amounts to an asset FRA. This method involves two entries: 1) recording the purchase as operating expense with 
all objects, 2) reallocating the amounts for all objects to an asset class.</p><p>First entry: To record the purchase and receipt of the vehicle on January 31, 2000.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Operating Expenses</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23,500</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B11A/B12A</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1261</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Operating Expenses</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>500</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B11A/B12A</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>0210</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR GST Refundable Advance</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1,680</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>13392</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>G111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8171</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accounts payable</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,680</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><p>Coding rationale - there is no change in the coding from entry 1, except for the use of the operating expense FRA instead 
of the asset FRA.</p><p>Second entry: To reallocate amounts for all objects.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Vehicle</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23,500</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16133</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B11A/B12A(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1261/3425</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Vehicle</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>500</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16133</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B11A/B12A(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>0210/3425</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Operating Expenses</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>500</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B11A/B12A</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>0210/3425</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Operating Expenses</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23,500</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B11A/B12A</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1261/3425</p></td></tr></table><p>Coding rationale - (*)There is no impact on the authority code unless it is moved to a capital appropriation (B14A). 
Object Coding: Departments may either use "3425 - Reallocation of expenditures/costs within a department" for all lines 
of the transaction or the asset and freight object codes used in entry 1. If more than one object is used, the same object 
must be used in the same amount for both the debit and credit sides of the entry. Note: if the transaction involves revenue 
credited to the vote, the economic object to use is "3717 - Recoveries of expenditures/costs within a department" for the 
credit side of the entry and "3425 - Reallocation of expenditures/costs within a department" for the debit side of the entry.</p><p>3) To record the amortization expense and the accumulated amortization at February 28, 2000.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Amortization Expense</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>200</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51433</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3451</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accumulated Amortization</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>200</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16233</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F311</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7061/7099</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> It is necessary to allocate the cost of the asset as an expense in a rational 
and systematic manner over those periods expected to benefit from the use of the asset. Using straight-line amortization, 
the monthly charge to amortization expense and accumulated amortization would be $200 ($24,000/10yrs = $2,400/year; $2,400/12mths 
= $200/month).</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> Expenditures for the acquisition were charged to an appropriation in the 
previous journal entry, therefore the appropriations are not affected in this journal entry. To assist with departmental 
reconciliations, F codes are used for these non-appropriated amounts. "F111 - Expenditures previously charged to appropriations/Amortization 
expenses for capital assets" is used for amortization expense and "F311 - Non-appropriated amounts added to or deducted 
from asset balances/ Increases (decreases) to accumulated amortization of capital assets" is used for accumulated amortization.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> As these are non-cash (non-expenditure) items, they have no effect on economic 
objects." 7061 - Accumulated amortization on capital assets" is used to capture accumulated amortization. Alternatively, 
"7099 - Net increase or decrease in other transactions" may also be used. "3451 - Amortization expense for capital assets" 
is used to capture amortization expense.</p><p>4) To record payment of vehicle on April 15, 2000.</p><p>See section on Accounts Payable for related entries.</p><h4>Scenario B - Betterment</h4><p>A betterment should be capitalized if the amount exceeds the department's threshold for betterments. The maximum threshold 
for betterments is $10,000. A department may choose a lower threshold. If the amount of the betterment is less the department's 
threshold for betterments, then the department should expense it.</p><p>The Department owns a building with an original cost of $250,000 and a useful life of 40 years. After 20 years the Department 
decides to do a major renovation that will increase the amount of usable space. The renovation work is contracted to one 
company and has a cost of $75,000. At this point the net book value of the building is $125,000 ($250,000/40yrs = $6,250/yr) 
($6,250/yrx20yrs = 125,000) ($250,000-$125,000 = $125,000)</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) Record the betterment</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Buildings</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>75000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16112</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B14A(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1340</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR GST Refundable Advance</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5250</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>13392</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>G111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8171</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accounts Payable</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>80,250</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale: </strong>Since the renovation is a betterment, it is added to the cost of the building 
i.e. capitalized as part of the building cost. The new value of the building is $200,000 ($125,000+$75,000). The amortization 
expense on the building will now increase to $10,000 ($200,000/20 years).</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> (*) In this example it is assumed this purchase would be charged to the 
capital vote. However, depending on the department and the asset purchased, the following authority codes could be used: 
B11A - Program Vote, B12A Operating Vote, or A131 Spending of amounts equivalent to proceeds from disposal of surplus Crown 
assets. There is no impact on the authority side for the accounts payable but as the system requires that a code be used, 
it would be "R300 - All other assets and liabilities"</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> As economic objects are recorded on an expenditure basis, the economic object 
is recorded at this point, and not when the cash (disbursement) is paid out. Economic object 1340 is used (in this example) 
since the renovation was on a building. If the details of the renovation expenditures are provided on the contractor's invoices 
and the department's system can accommodate the use of more than one economic object per asset class, it would be preferable 
to use the different economic object codes depending on the nature of the purchase (as done in Scenario C). "6299 - Net 
Increase or Decrease to Other Liability Accounts" is used to record the accrual of the amount owing.</p><h4>Scenario C - Betterment - Work Managed by Department</h4><p>Same details as in Scenario B except the department is contracting the work. The cost of the betterment include: wages, 
freight, architect fees, rentals of machinery; materials, equipment and fixtures. An alternative entry involving the detailed 
re-allocation of all objects is shown for the second and third entries.</p><p>1) Record the $25,000 of expenses incurred during the first month</p><table class="table table-bordered the entry.</p><h4>Scenario D - Disposal via Sale of Tangible Capital Asset</h4><p>On May 1, 2000, the Department purchased informatics-hardware for $32,000 with an estimated service life of five years 
and an estimated residual value after five years of $2,000. The Department uses straight-line amortization and decides to 
sell the asset on November 1, 2004, for $8,000.</p><p>Alternative entries using a suspense account for proceeds from asset sales, and involving two entries in each case are 
shown below.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1a) Record the disposal of the asset and related gain in November 2004.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Cash in the hands of the dept awaiting deposit to RG</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11125</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5299</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Accumulated Amortization - informatics hardware</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>27,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16222</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4843</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Informatics hardware</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>32,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16122</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4843</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Gain from disposal of equipment</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>42411</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4843</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale: </strong>The Department must record the proceeds received ($8,000) by debiting Cash in 
the hands of the department awaiting deposit to the RG. The equipment and related accumulated amortization must be written 
off the books. In this case the net of these three items results in a gain which will be credited to the non-tax revenue 
FRA. The accumulated amortization is $27,000 and is calculated as follows ($32,000-2,000 = $30,000) ($30,000/60 mths = $500/mth) 
(54 mths x $500 = $27,000)</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> There is no authority impact for the cash received, R300 is used. "D321- 
Proceeds from disposal of crown assets" is used for the remaining debits and credits ($27,000-$32,000-$3,000) as it reflects 
the allocation of the proceeds of $8,000 received by the Department.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> To record the net impact on Cash Accounts, 5299 would be used. As economic 
objects are recorded on an expenditure basis, one object should be used to record the proceeds from sale. "4843 - Sales 
of surplus Crown assets to outside parties".</p><p><strong>Alternative entries:</strong> There is an alternative method to record the sale of an asset that uses two entries 
with a suspense account in the middle</p><p>First entry:</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Cash in the hands of the dept awaiting deposit to RG</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11125</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5299</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Suspense acct: Proceeds from Asset Sale</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21627</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4843</p></td></tr></table><p>Second entry:</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Suspense acct: contra proceeds</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21627</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F999</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Accumulated Amortization - informatics hardware</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>27,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16222</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F999</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Gain from disposal of equipment</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>42411</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F999</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Informatics hardware</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>32,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16122</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F999</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr></table><p>Rationale: The FRAs used are the same with the exception of the addition of a suspense account (FRA 21627). All the authority 
and object information are in the first entry, while the second entry provides the accrual accounting data, while having 
a nil impact on the authority and object information. To ensure a nil effect on economic objects, the same code, "7099-Net 
Increase or Decrease in Other Transactions" or "3425-Reallocation of expenditures/costs within a department" should be used 
throughout the transaction.</p><p>1b) Assuming the circumstance is the same as above except the Department decides to sell the asset for $3,000, on November 
1, 2004. Record the disposal of the asset and the related loss.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DRCash in the hands of the Dept awaiting deposit to RG</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11125</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5299</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Accumulated Amortization - informatics hardware</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>27,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16222</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4843</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Loss on disposal of physical assets</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>2,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51511</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4843</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Informatics hardware</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>32,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16122</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4843</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale: </strong>The Department must record the proceeds received ($3,000) by debiting Cash in 
the hands of the department awaiting deposit to the RG. The equipment and related accumulated amortization must be written 
off the books. In this case the net of these three items results in a loss which will be debited to an expense FRA.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> There is no authority impact for cash received, but the system requires 
that a code be used. In this case R300 is used. "D321- Proceeds from disposal of crown assets" is used for the remaining 
debits and credits ($27,000-$32,000+$2,000) as it reflects the allocation of the proceeds of $3,000 received by the Department.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> As economic objects are recorded on an expenditure basis, one object is used 
to record the proceeds from sale "4843-Sales of surplus Crown assets to outside parties". To record the net impact on Cash 
Accounts, 5299 would be used.</p><p><strong>Alternative entries:</strong> There is an alternative method to record the sale of an asset which uses two entries 
with a suspense account in the middle</p><p>First entry:</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Cash in the hands of the dept awaiting deposit to RG</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11125</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5299</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Suspense acct: Proceeds from Asset Sale</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21627</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4843</p></td></tr></table><p>Second entry:</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Asset Sale - Contra Proceeds awaiting deposit to RG</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21627</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F999</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Accumulated Amortization - informatics hardware</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>27,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16222</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F999</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Loss on disposal of physical assets</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>2,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51511</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F999</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Informatics hardware</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>32,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16122</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F999</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr></table><p>Rationale: The FRAs used are the same with the exception of the addition of a suspense account (FRA 21627). All the authority 
and object information are in the first entry, while the second entry provides the accrual accounting data, while having 
a nil impact on the authority and object information. To ensure a nil effect on economic objects, the same code, "7099 - 
Net Increase or Decrease in Other Transactions" or "3425 - Reallocation of expenditures/costs within a department" should 
be used throughout the transaction.</p><h4>Scenario E - Disposal via Trade-In</h4><p>It should be noted that there are restrictions on what moveable assets departments can trade-in (e.g. passenger cars, 
wagons and light commercial trucks) and whether departments can trade these assets for similar or different types of assets 
(see the <em>Material Management Policy</em> and <em>Motor Vehicle Policy: </em><a href="/pubs_pol/dcgpubs/materielmanage/siglist_eng.asp">/pubs_pol/dcgpubs/materielmanage/siglist_eng.asp</a>).</p><p>The Department trades in an old piece of research equipment for a new piece of research equipment. The old equipment 
has an accumulated amortization of $7,000 and an original cost of $8,000. The department receives $600 on the trade in. 
The new equipment has a value of $10,000.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) Record the trade-in</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><td class="alignTopRight">
 </td><td class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></td></tr><tr><td class="alignTop"><p>DR Other equipment (new)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>10,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16129</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B14A(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1219</p></td></tr><tr><td class="alignTop"><p>DR Accumulated Amortization equipment (old)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16229</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4843</p></td></tr><tr><td class="alignTop"><p>DR Loss on disposal of physical assets</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>400</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51511</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4843</p></td></tr><tr><td class="alignTop"><p>DR GST refundable advance account</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>658</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>13392</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>G111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8171</p></td></tr><tr><td class="alignTop"><p>CR Other equipment (old)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16129</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4843</p></td></tr><tr><td class="alignTop"><p>CR Accounts Payable</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>10,058</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale: </strong>The equipment (old) and related accumulated amortization must be written off the 
books. Because the Department received $600 for the trade-in, the loss on the disposal of the trade-in is $400 ($8,000-$7,000-$600). 
The equipment (new) is recorded at its original purchase price and the amount payable to the vendor is the difference between 
the purchase price of the equipment (new) and the $600 received for the trade in, plus GST of $658. GST is payable on the 
net purchase price of the equipment (7% of $9,400).</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> (*) In this example it is assumed this purchase (equipment (new)) would 
be charged to the capital vote. However, depending on the department and the asset purchased, the following authority codes 
could be used: B11A - Program Vote, B12A Operating Vote, or A131 Spending of amounts equivalent to proceeds from disposal 
of surplus Crown assets. There is no impact on the authority side for the accounts payable, "R300- All other assets and 
liabilities" would be used. "D321 - Proceeds from disposal of crown assets" is used ($7,000+$400-$8,000) to reflect proceeds 
of $600 received by the Department for the old equipment. Since GST is not to be charged to a departmental appropriation, 
it is set up as an advance under a special authority, G111.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> The economic object is recorded at this point since objects are recorded on 
an expenditure basis. Economic object 1219 is used to record the purchase of the new equipment - other machinery parts. 
" 6299 - Net Increase or Decrease to Other Liability Accounts" is used to establish the payable for the amount owing. The 
GST is reflected by using "8171 - Payment of GST on purchases". "4843 - Sales of surplus Crown assets to outside parties" 
is used in the remainder of this entry, because it relates to all the proceeds received for the asset being sold.</p><p>2) Transfer of funds (optional entry)</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop">  </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Other equipment (new)</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>600</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16129</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>A131</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Other equipment (new)</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>600</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16129</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B14*</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> The purpose of this entry is purely for authority purposes, there is no effect 
on FRAs. The same FRA is debited and credited.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> The proceeds from the trade-in of $600 are credited to whichever B code 
the purchase was charged to. In this way, the charge to the appropriation is the net cost of the asset. This entry is optional 
depending on how departments choose to use the funds related to A131 - Spending of amounts equivalent to proceeds from disposal 
of surplus crown assets.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> The purpose of this entry is purely for authority purposes, there is no effect 
on economic objects. "7099 - Net increase or decrease in other transactions" is used on both sides of the transaction.</p><h4>Scenario F - Write-off of Tangible Capital Asset</h4><p>Informatics hardware originally costing $120,000 with a useful life of 5 years has a $60,000 accumulated amortization 
balance on April 1, 2000. It is amortized at $2,000 per month. In July a fire caused substantial damage to the equipment. 
The Department decides the equipment has no future benefits and should be written off immediately.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) Write-off (bringing the value of the capital asset to zero)</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop">  </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Accumulated Amortization - informatics hardware</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>66,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16222</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F351</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Loss on disposal of physical assets</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>54,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51511</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F351</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Informatics hardware</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>120,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16122</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F351</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale: </strong>The equipment and related accumulated amortization (after adding an additional 
$6,000 in amortization expense to the accumulated amortization for the informatics hardware in year 2000) must be written 
off the books. The net result of these items will result in a loss of $54,000. FRA 51511 is used as the department has disposed 
of the asset. FRA 51733 "Losses on write-offs and write-downs" would be used if the asset continues to be used (see Scenario 
G).</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> This is strictly an accrual accounting transaction. There is no impact on 
the authorities as the appropriation was charged when the asset was purchased. In order to ensure there is a nil effect 
on authorities, the same authority code is used for all debits and credits. In this case "F351 - Write off of Capital Assets 
was used."</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> This is strictly an accrual accounting transaction with no impact on the economic 
objects, as there is no impact on the economy. The economic objects were affected when the asset was purchased. To ensure 
a nil effect on economic objects, the same code, "7099 - Net Increase or Decrease in Other Transactions" or "3425 - Reallocation 
of expenditures/costs within a department" should be used throughout the transaction.</p><h4>Scenario G - Write-down of Tangible Capital Asset</h4><p>Internally developed software put into operation a year ago has a cost of $400,000 and accumulated amortization of $40,000. 
The department determines that the software will not provide the full benefits expected (e.g. the software cannot handle 
the volume of processing required and additional software will have to be purchased to supplement it). The department determines 
that the cost of the software should be reduced by $100,000 to reflect the decline in the asset's value (this could be the 
amount of the additional costs required to supplement the software).</p><p>Note: other reasons supporting the need for the write-down of an asset can be found in PS 3150.36.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) Write-down</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop">  </th><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Losses on write-downs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>100,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51733</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F351</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accumulated amortization: informatics software</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>100,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16223</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F351</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099/3425</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale: </strong>FRA 51733 "Losses on write-downs" would be used as the asset continues to be used. 
The credit is to accumulated amortization to reflect the decrease in the net book value of the asset.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> This is strictly an accrual accounting transaction. There is no impact on 
the authorities as the appropriation was charged when the asset was purchased. In order to ensure there is a nil effect 
on authorities, the same authority code is used for the debit and credit. In this case "F351 - Write off of Capital Assets 
was used."</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> This is strictly an accrual accounting transaction with no impact on the economic 
objects, as there is no impact on the economy. The economic objects were affected when the asset was purchased. To ensure 
a nil effect on economic objects, the same code "7099 - Net Increase or Decrease in Other Transactions" or "3425 - Reallocation 
of expenditures/costs within a department" should be used throughout the transaction.</p><h4>Departmental Financial Statement Presentation and Disclosure Requirements</h4><p>As per TBAS 1.2, for each category of capital asset disclose original cost, additions, disposals, write-downs, accumulated 
amortization, amortization, and net book value on the Schedule of Capital Assets in the departmental financial statements. 
Also, for those capital assets where the net book value is already nil, the original historic cost should be disclosed in 
the notes to the financial statements as an indication of their existence.</p><h5>3.5.1.1 Capital Leases</h5><p>A lease is a contractual agreement between a lessor and a lessee that gives the lessee the right to use specific property 
owned by the lessor for a specific period of time in return for generally periodic cash payments.</p><p>If a government department is the lessee, the lease is classified for accounting purposes as either an operating lease 
or a capital lease. The department would classify a lease as capital if any one of the following conditions are met:</p><ul><li>Is there a transfer of ownership?</li><li>Is there a bargain purchase option?</li><li>Is the lease term greater than or equal to 75% of the asset's economic life?</li><li>Is the present value of payments greater than or equal to 90% of the fair value of the asset?</li></ul><p>If a government department is the lessor, then the leases would be classified for accounting purposes as either:</p><ul><li>Operating leases; or</li><li>Direct financing leases or sales-type leases</li></ul><h4>References</h4><ul><li>CICA 3065 (particularly CICA 3065.21-26)</li></ul><h4>Scenario A - Department enters into Capital Lease agreement as Lessee</h4><p>Lessor Company and the Department sign a lease agreement that calls for Lessor Company to lease informatics equipment 
to the Department beginning January1, 2005. The lease contains the following terms and provisions.</p><ol><li>The term of the lease is five years, and the lease agreement is non-cancellable, requiring equal payments of $25,981.62 
  at the beginning of each year (annuity due basis) plus GST.</li><li>The equipment has a fair value at the inception of the lease of $100,000, an estimated economic life of five years, 
  and no residual value at the end of the 5 years.</li><li>The Department pays all the executory costs directly except for maintenance costs of $2,000 per year, which are included 
  in the annual payments to the lessor.</li><li>The lease contains no renewal options and the equipment reverts to Lessor Company at the termination of the lease.</li><li>The Department amortizes similar equipment it owns on a straight-line basis.</li><li>Lessor Company set the annual rental to ensure a rate of return on its investments of 10% per year; the Department 
  is aware of this fact. In the event that the Department did not know the lessor's rate of return, the Department would 
  use the CRF lending rate at the time the agreement is signed.</li></ol><p>The lease meets the criteria for classification as a capital lease because (1) the lease term of five years, being equal 
to the equipment's estimated economic life of five years, satisfies the 75% test; or because (2) the present value of the 
minimum lease payments ($100, 000 as computed below) exceeds 90% of the fair value of the property ($100,000).</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) To record the capital lease on January 1, 2005.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Informatics Equip-Capital Leases (asset)</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>100,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16622</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Informatics Equip-Capital Lease (obligation)</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>100,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>24222</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> The asset value and the amount of the obligation are recorded at the beginning 
of the lease term at the present value of the lease payments, excluding the portion relating to executory costs.</p><p>The minimum lease payments are $119,908.10 ($23,981.62 x 5) and the amount capitalized as leased assets is $100,000, 
the present value of the minimum lease payments is determined as follows:</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><td class="alignTop"><p>Capitalized amount</p></td><td class="alignTop"><p>= ($25981.62-$2 000) x present value of an annuity due of $1 for 5 periods at 10%.</p></td></tr><tr><td class="alignTop">
 </td><td class="alignTop"><p>= $23981.62 x 4.16986</p></td></tr><tr><td class="alignTop">
 </td><td class="alignTop"><p>= $100000</p></td></tr></table><p>The lessor's implicit interest rate of 10% is used instead of the lessee's incremental borrowing rate of 11% because 
(1) it is lower, and (2) the lessee has knowledge of it.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> This is strictly an accrual entry. The appropriations are not affected at 
this point. The appropriation is charged only when the lease, interest payments and executory payments are made. "R300 - 
All other assets and liabilities" is used here for both sides of the entry.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> As economic objects are recorded on an expenditure basis, the economic object 
is not recorded at this point but when the lease payment is made. "7099-Net increase or decrease in other transactions" 
is used. "6299-Net Increases or Decreases in Other Liability Accounts" is used to establish the accrual of the amount owing.</p><p>2) To record the first lease payment on January 1, 2005.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop">  </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Operating Expenses (executory costs)</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>2,000.00</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>(**)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>0525</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Informatics Equip-Capital Lease (obligation)</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23,981.62</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>24222</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>(**)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1221</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR GST refundable advance</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1,818.71</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>13392</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>G111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8171</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accounts Payable</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>27,800.33</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> The first lease payment of $23,981.62 represents a reduction of the principal 
of the lease obligation. There is no interest paid out at this point. At year-end the expense is accrued, (see journal entry 
3) below. The executory costs are coded to operating expenses. The Department must record a payable for the amount owing 
of $25,981.62 plus GST of $1,818.71.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> (**) In this example, it is assumed this lease payment and operating expense 
would be charged to the capital vote -B14A. However, depending on the departmental appropriations, the following authority 
codes could be used: B11A - Program Vote, B12A Operating Vote, and A131 Spending of amounts equivalent to proceeds from 
disposal of surplus Crown assets. As there is no impact on the authorities for accounts payable, the code would be "R300- 
All other assets and liabilities" since the system requires that a code be used. Since GST is not to be charged to a departmental 
appropriation, it is set up as an advance under a special authority, G111.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> At this point expenditures are made for the executory costs and lease costs. 
Therefore economic objects are affected. In this case, "0525-Rental of computer equipment" is used for the executory costs 
and "1221-Voice communication equipment" is used for the lease payment. "6299-Net Increase or Decrease to Other Liability 
Accounts" is used establish an accounts payable. The GST must be reflected by using "8171-Payment of GST on purchases".</p><p>Each rental payment of $25,981.62 consists of three elements: (1) a reduction in the principal of the lease obligation; 
(2) a financing cost (interest expense); and (3) executory costs. The total financing cost or interest expense over the 
term of the lease is the difference between the present value of the lease payments ($100,000) and the actual cash disbursed, 
net of executory costs ($119,908.10), or $19,908.10. <strong>Note:</strong> In the journal entry 2) above no portion of 
the 23,981.62 relates to interest expense. The interest is accrued at the end of the year, (see journal entry 3) below) 
and is paid in the beginning of the following year (see 5) below).</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><caption><strong>Lease Amortization Schedule<br></br>
  (Annuity Due Basis)</strong></caption><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>Date</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>Annual Lease Payment</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>Interest (10%) on Unpaid Obligation</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>Reduction of Lease Obligation</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>Balance of Lease Obligation</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop">

below).</p><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> The interest expense over the term of the lease is the difference between the 
present value of the lease payments and the actual cash disbursed for the lease payment. The interest expense is a function 
of the outstanding obligation. $7,601.84 = ((100,000-23,981.62) x 10%). It is necessary to set up an accrual for the three 
months Jan 01, 2005 to March 31, 2005 since the department's fiscal year ends on March 31. This would amount to $1,900.46 
($7,601.84 / 12mths x 3mths) interest owing. The Accrued Interest Payable on Capital Leases would be reversed in the following 
year. Please note: if material, the interest expense would recorded on a monthly basis.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> This is strictly an accrual transaction. The appropriation is not affected 
at this time. The charge to the appropriation occurs when the interest is actually paid out as part of the periodic lease 
payment. Therefore, it is necessary to use an F code. For the interest expense portion "F129 - Expenses to be charged later 
to appropriations/Other amounts to be charged later". Accrued interest payable on capital leases does not affect the appropriations, 
thus "R300 - Total amounts of all other assets and liabilities" would be used.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> This is strictly an accrual transaction and there is no effect on economic 
objects. "3469- Charges to other liability account" or "7099- Net increase of decrease in other transactions" should be 
used. To establish the payable "6299-Net Increase or Decrease to Other Liability Accounts" should be used.</p><p>3b) To record the interest expense for the period between April 01, 2005 and Dec. 31, 2005.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop">  </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Interest Component on capital lease pymt</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,701.38</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51713</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F129</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3469/7099</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accrued Interest Payable on Capital leases</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,701.38</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21154</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><p>Accrued interest payable on capital leases would be reversed and put into Accounts Payable on January 1, 2006, see 5) 
below.</p><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> It is necessary to set up an accrual for nine months April 01, 2005 to December 
31, 2005. This would amount to $5,701.38 ($7,601.84 / 12mths x 9mths) interest owing. The accrued interest payable on capital 
leases would be reversed in the following year. Please note: If material the interest expense would recorded on a monthly 
basis.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> Same as 3a).</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> Same as 3a).</p><p>4) To record the amortization expense and accumulated amortization for the month.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop">  </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Amortization Expense - Infor Equip (leased)</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1,667</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51422</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3451</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accumulated Amortization - Infor Equip (leased)</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1,667</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16722</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F311</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7061/7099</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> The Department should record amortization expense and accumulated amortization 
as per the Department's normal amortization policy (e.g. straight-line method). $100,000/5years= $20,000/yr $20,000/12mths=$1,666.67/mth</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> Since the expenditure for the acquisition was already charged to an appropriation 
in previous journal entries, the appropriations are not affected. F codes would be used to assist with departmental reconciliations. 
"F111 - Amortization expenses for capital assets" is used for amortization expense and "F311 - Increases (decreases) to 
accumulated amortization of capital assets" is used for accumulated amortization.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> These non-cash items have no effect on economic objects."7061- Accumulated 
amortization on capital assets" or "7099 - Net increase or decrease in other transactions" is used to capture accumulated 
amortization. "3451 - Amortization expense for capital assets" is used to capture amortization expense.</p><p>5) To record the lease payment and to charge the interest expense to the appropriation on January 1, 2006.</p><div class="indent1"><p>5a) To record the lease payment on January 1, 2006</p></div><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th rationale:</strong> The recording of the lease payment results in a reduction of the lease obligation 
and the recording of a payable to reflect an amount owing to the lessor. The accrued interest charges are reversed and recorded 
as an accounts payable to reflect an amount owing the lessor as well. The executory costs are charged to an operating expense.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> (**) In this example, it is assumed this lease payment and operating expenses 
would be charged to the capital vote B14A. However, depending on the departmental appropriations, the following authority 
codes could be used: B11A - Program Vote, B12A Operating Vote, and A131 Spending of amounts equivalent to proceeds from 
disposal of surplus Crown assets. As there in no impact on authorities for accounts payable and accrued interest payable 
on capital leases, R300 would be used, as the system requires that a code be input.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> "6299-Net Increase or Decrease to Other Liability Accounts" is used to record 
the net impact on other liabilities. At this point expenditures are incurred for the executory costs and the lease costs, 
therefore economic objects are affected. In this case "0525-Rental of computer equipment" and "1221-Voice communication 
equipment" are used.</p><div class="indent1"><p>5b) To charge the interest expense to the appropriation on January 1, 2006</p></div><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Interest Component on capital lease pymt</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7,601.84</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51713</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>(***)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3252</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Interest Component on capital lease pymt</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7,601.84</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51713</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F159</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> This transaction does not affect accruals only appropriations. However, the system 
requires that FRA codes be input. To ensure a nil effect on departmental FRAs, it would be necessary to debit and credit 
the same FRA code for the same amount.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> (***) In this example, it is assumed the lease payment and operating expense 
would be charged to the capital vote B14A, therefore the interest expense would be charged to the same vote. This is not 
considered to be a public debt charge. However, depending on the department, the following authority codes could be used: 
B11A - Program Vote, B12A Operating Vote, and A131 Spending of amounts equivalent to proceeds from disposal of surplus Crown 
assets. Since this transaction is required to affect an appropriation, only one side of the transaction will get charged. 
As a result it is necessary to use an F code on the other (credit) side of the transaction. In this case, "F159 - Other 
expenses not being charged to appropriations at the same time" is used.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> The economic object "3252- Interest administration or service charges, and 
other penalty charges" would be used to record the interest expense. The credit entry would be to "7099 - Net Increase or 
Decrease in Other Transactions".</p><h4>Scenario B - Department purchases leased equipment at the end of the lease term.</h4><p>Please note that same terms and conditions apply in this Scenario as in Scenario A except that the Department purchases 
the leased equipment at the end of the lease term for $5,000. (The estimated useful life has been increased by 2 years)</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>Journal entries 1 to 5 - see Scenario A above.</p><p>6) To record the purchase of the leased equipment at end of lease term for $5,000.</p><table class="widthFull"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Informatics Equipment</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>100,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16122</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F351</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7099</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Informatics Equipment</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16122</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>(****)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1221</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Accumulated Amortiz -
