This amount of $100,000 must be reversed 
in the new year. The new year expense of $50,000 is the net amount charged to salaries and wages expense. The total of $150,000 
is charged directly to the Payroll Control Account (2b).</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> In entry 1) the salaries of $100,000 were charged to B11A(*) or B12A or 
B14A. In entry 2a) the appropriation is being credited for the same amount (due to reversal requirements) and in entry 2b) 
the $150,000 be charged to the appropriation. The net result is that appropriation will only charged for $50,000, which 
is the new year overtime. Please note that the credit to the appropriation is so that the new year appropriation is not 
over-charged when the payment of salaries is made in the new year. Since accrued salaries and wages (which is a payable) 
has no impact on appropriations, R300 is used. Control accounts are zero filled, since they do not impact on appropriations.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> Entry 2a) is a reversal of entry 1). The payment of $150,000 in overtime is charged 
to "0105 - Civilian overtime". "6299- Net Increase or Decrease to Other Liability accounts" is used to indicate the reduction 
of the accrued payable. All RG interface Control Accounts are zero filled (0000), with the exception of I/S Control Accounts, 
at the object level.</p><h4>Scenario D - Compensatory leave accruals at year-end</h4><p>A Department accrues compensatory leave accruals of $50,000 on March 31, 2003. This amount does not need to be reversed 
out in the new year. The Department cashes out $25,000 of old year compensatory leave in the new year.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) Old Year Accrual of $50,000</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Salaries and wages</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>50,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51311</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F125</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3461</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Allowance for time-off in lieu</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>50,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21414</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F419</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7023</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> At the end of the year the Department should recognize the expense of time-off 
in lieu of payment owed to its employees. As the liability is for future time-off and not a future payment, the credit is 
to an allowance account rather than accounts payable.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> This entry does not affect appropriations as no cash payment will result 
from this transaction hence F codes are used. "F125 - Allowances set up for compensatory leave" and "F419 - Charges to other 
accruals and allowances" are used.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> "3461 - Allowance for vacation pay and similar employee benefit" and "7023 - Allowance 
for employee benefits" are used for object codes.</p><p>2) Cashing out of old year compensatory leave of $25,000</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Allowance for time-off in lieu</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21414</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B11A(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>0105</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Pay control account</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>63XXX</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>0000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>0000</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> In the new year, $25,000 of compensatory leave is cashed out to employees. Since 
the expense related to the time-off was recognized last year, the debit is to the allowance account. The amount owed is 
credited to the pay control account.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> The cashing out of compensatory leave will have an impact on the current 
year's authorities. In this case, B11A(*) was used however other authorities including B12A or B14A (if the salary costs 
of an employee are being capitalized) could also be appropriate. Control accounts are zero filled for authority purposes.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> "0105 - Civilian overtime" is used to the cashing out of compensatory leave. Control 
accounts are zero filled for object purposes.</p><p><strong>Note:</strong> A department may choose to reverse entry 1) at the beginning of the year if their system cannot 
process entry 2). In this case, the cashing out of old year compensatory leave in the new year would be debited to expense 
rather than the allowance. However, the allowance would need to be set up again every month (if significant).</p><h4>Scenario E - Year-end annual leave accruals</h4><p>A Department accrues annual leave not taken of $1,000,000 at year-end. In the new year, pays out $25,000 for an employee 
who leaves the Government.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) Old Year Accrual of $1,000,000</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Salaries and wages</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1,000,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51311</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F121</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3461</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Allowance for vacation pay</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1,000,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21411</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F411</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7023</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> At the end of the year the Department should recognize the expense of vacation 
time owed to its employees. As the liability is for future time-off and not a future payment, the credit is to an allowance 
account rather than accounts payable.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> This entry does not affect appropriations as no cash payment will result 
from this transaction hence F codes are used. "F121 - Allowances set up for vacation leave" and "F411 - Changes to allowance 
for vacation pay" are used.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> "3461 - Allowance for vacation pay and similar employee benefit" and "7023 - Allowance 
for employee benefits" are used for object codes.</p><p>2) Cashing out of vacation pay of $25,000</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Allowance for vacation pay</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21411</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B11A(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>0104</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Pay control account</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>63XXX</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>0000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>0000</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> In the new year, $25,000 of vacation pay is cashed out to an employee. Since the 
expense related to the vacation time owed was recognized last year, the debit is to the allowance account. The amount owed 
is credited to the pay control account.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> The cashing out of compensatory leave will have an impact on the current 
year's authorities. In this case, B11A(*) was used however other authorities including B12A or B14A (if the salary costs 
of an employee are being capitalized) could also be appropriate. Control accounts are zero filled for authority purposes.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> "0104 - Civilian holiday pay in lieu of leave" is used for the cashing out of vacation 
leave. Control accounts are zero filled for object purposes.</p><h4>Scenario F - Year-end accrual of retroactive salary settlements</h4><p>Collective agreements have been ratified and signed on March 31, and result in a retroactive salary settlement of $500,000 
outstanding at year-end. In the new year, pays out the $500,000 in addition to an additional $100,000.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) Old Year Accrual of $500,000</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Salaries and wages</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>500,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51311</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B11A(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3469/7099</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accrued Salaries and Wages</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>500,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21112</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><div class="indent1"><p>(See section on Accounts Payable for the entries required for settlement of accounts payable)</p></div><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> At the end of the year the Department needs to accrue the retroactive salary settlement

employee are being capitalized. Since accrued salaries and wages have no impact on appropriations, R300 is used.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> "6299- Net Increase or Decrease to Other Liability accounts" should be used to indicate

wages FRA is charged to "0107 - Civilian severance pay and termination benefits. "6299- Net Increase or Decrease to Other
