filled (0000), with the exception of I/S Control Accounts, at the object level.</p><h4>Departmental Financial Statement Presentation and Disclosure Requirements</h4><p>Salaries will be recorded as expenses in the Department's Statement of Operations. Accrued salaries and wages and related 
allowances will appear as liabilities in the department's Statement of Financial Position.</p></section><section anchor="7.4" title="7.4 Services Provided Without Charge"><h4>Introduction</h4><p>In some instances government departments provide services to other government departments free of charge. Examples of 
these services included:</p><ul><li>accommodation provided by Public Works and Government Services;</li><li>contributions covering employer's share of employees' insurance premiums and costs paid by Treasury Board;</li><li>salary and associated costs of legal services provided by Department of Justice;</li><li>audit services provided by the Office of the Auditor General; etc.</li></ul><p>Disclosure requirements will vary depending on whether the Department's financial statements are audited.</p><p><strong><em>Department that DO NOT have Audited Financial Statements</em></strong></p><p>Services provided without charge by other government departments are not recorded as operating expenses. However, departments 
that do receive services without charge must disclose the nature of these services in note to the financial statements. 
More specifically, the details would be found in note 2, of TBAS 1.2 "Departmental and Agency Financial Statements". An 
example of what would be required is as follows:</p><p>"<em>Services provided without charge by other government departments are not recorded as operating expenses. The following 
are the more significant types of services provided without charge: accommodation provided by Public Works and Government 
Services; contributions covering employer' share of employees' insurance premiums and costs paid by Treasury Board; salary 
and associated costs of legal services provided by Department of Justice; audit services provided by the Office of the Auditor 
General; etc</em>.<strong><br></br>
(Departments are to include estimates of the amounts involved).</strong>"</p><p><strong><em>Departments that have Audited Financial Statements</em></strong></p><p>Services without charge are not to be reflected in the CFMRS Trial Balance sent to the Receiver General. In other words, 
they are not formally recorded as operating expenses. However, an adjustment is done to the trial balance for financial 
statement purposes. The amount that represents services without charge is added to operating expenses in the Department's 
Statement of Operations. Since the amounts for services without charge are included in the Statement of Operations and NOT 
in the CFMRS Trial Balance, they must be eliminated through the Net Asset position of the Statement of Financial Position. 
As well note disclosure of the nature of these services is required. An example of what would be required is as follows:</p><p><em>"The following are the more significant types of services provided without charge: accommodation provided by Public 
Works and Government Services; contributions covering employer' share of employees' insurance premiums and costs paid by 
Treasury Board; salary and associated costs of legal services provided by Department of Justice; audit services provided 
by the Office of the Auditor General; etc</em>."</p><p>An excerpt from the Statement of Financial Position of Department X will demonstrate the above point.</p><p><em>Net Assets</em></p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"><p><em>Net assets, beginning of the year</em></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><em>$160,038</em></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p><em>Net operating results</em></p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p><em>(326,098)</em></p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p><em>Services provided without charge</em></p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p><em>25,572</em></p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p><em>Net cash provided by government</em></p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p><em>285,110</em></p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p><em>Net asset, end of year</em></p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p><em>$144,622</em></p></td></tr></table><h4>References</h4><ul><li>TBAS 1.2 Departmental and Agency Financial Statements</li></ul></section></chapter><chapter anchor="8" title="8.0 Control Accounts"><h4>Introduction</h4><p>Control accounts are akin to a bank account. Since Departments do not have bank accounts, control accounts have been 
established that function like a bank account in the private sector. The major difference between these control accounts 
and bank accounts is that control accounts get closed into Net Assets/Liabilities at year end after all other closings have 
been done. See Net Assets/Liabilities section of the manual for example.</p><p>The authority code used for all control accounts is 0000.</p><p>At the object level, all RG interface control accounts are zero filled (0000), with the exception of I/S Control Accounts. 
Please see the <a href="http://www.pwgsc.gc.ca/recgen/gw-coa/0405/toc-e.html">Chart of Accounts</a></p><p>The control accounts are as follows:</p><p>61DDD Cash Payment Control Accounts<br></br>
62DDD Cash Deposit Control Accounts<br></br>
63DDD Payroll Control Accounts<br></br>
64DDD I.S. Debit Control Accounts<br></br>
65DDD I.S. Credit Control Accounts<br></br>
66DDD Cash Payments Control Accounts in U.S. dollars</p><p>DDD represents the Department number.</p><p>For examples showing control accounts, please see the following sections of the manual:</p><p>Cash<br></br>
Accounts Payable<br></br>
Respendable versus Non-Respendable Revenue</p><h4>References</h4><ul><li><a href="http://www.pwgsc.gc.ca/recgen/gw-coa/0405/toc-e.html">Chart of Accounts for the Financial Reporting Authority for Fiscal Year 2004-2005</a></li></ul><h4>Departmental Financial Statement Presentation and Disclosure Requirements</h4><p>Since control accounts get closed into Net assets/Liabilities, they are reflected in the Net Assets portion of the statements 
of the financial statements.</p></chapter><chapter anchor="9" title="9.0 Other Accounting Policies and Disclosures"><section anchor="9.1" title="9.1 Specified Purpose Accounts"><h4>Introduction</h4><p>Departments and agencies receive, for various reasons, money that must be accounted for separately in the Accounts of 
Canada. In some cases, the enabling legislation requires that revenues be earmarked, and that related payments and expenditures 
be charged against such revenues. In other cases, money is received for a specified purpose and is recorded in a SPA for 
authority purposes but treated like deferred revenue (a liability) for accrual accounting purposes. SPAs are classified 
either as consolidated SPAs, non-consolidated SPAs or deferred revenue SPAs in the financial statements of the Government 
of Canada.</p><ol><li>Consolidated SPAs are a restricted category of budgetary revenue and expenditures. These SPAs are consolidated as 
  the purpose for which they are established is similar in nature to departmental activities. The consolidation of these 
  accounts implies that the funds received from outside parties do not remain the property of the contributors, and the 
  transactions in the account are essentially government revenues and expenditures. Moneys received are credited to revenue 
  in the year received. The net revenue/deficit balance of these SPAs are reported separately as part of the accumulated 
  deficit (see note 5 of financial statements). Details of consolidated SPAs are presented in section 4 - Consolidated Accounts 
  of the Public Accounts. Consolidated SPAs include: budgetary insurance accounts, fees and levies imposed by statute and 
  earmarked for a special purpose, and court awards that have been specifically earmarked by the court. The principal portion 
  of an endowment is also accounted for as a consolidated SPA. The balances of these accounts appear in Financial Reporting 
  Accounts in the 312XX range. Each consolidated SPA has its own specific authority code.</li><li>Non-consolidated SPAs represent a financial obligation of the Government of Canada, either to the parties from whom 
  the funds were received, or in situations where a statutory or a contractual obligation must be recorded. Non-consolidated 
  SPAs appear as liabilities in the accounts of Canada. Details of these SPAs are presented in section 6 - Interest- Bearing 
  Debt of the Public Accounts. The expenditures and revenues of non-consolidated SPAs are recorded as decreases and increases 
  to the liability account and are not recorded as revenues and expenses of the Government of Canada. These SPAs include: 
  deposit and trust accounts; pension, insurance and death benefits accounts; federal-provincial arrangements; and certain 
  cost-sharing and joint project arrangements. The balances of these accounts appear in the Financial Reporting Accounts 
  in the 226XX, 232XX and 2344X accounts. Each non-consolidated SPA has its own specific authority code.</li><li>Deferred Revenues SPAs represent an obligation of the Government of Canada to spend funds received for their specified 
  purpose. The expenditures and revenues of the SPA are included in the revenues and expenditures of the Government of Canada 
  once the specified purpose has been completed. These SPAs include: bequests, donations, and gifts received for a specified 
  purpose; pre-payments for unspecified goods and services; the interest earned on endowment funds; and certain cost-sharing 
  and joint project arrangements. Note that up until the 2000-2001 year-end, bequests, donations, gifts, and the interest 
  earned on endowment funds were accounted for as consolidated SPAs. However, starting with fiscal year 2001-2002, the classification 
  of these SPAs has bee changed to Deferred Revenues SPAs to comply with Generally Accepted Accounting Principles. The balances 
  of these accounts appear in the Financial Reporting Account 23451 - Deferred revenues - SPAs. Each deferred revenue SPA 
  has its own specific authority code.</li></ol><p>The following types of SPAs will be examined in this section:</p><ul><li>Prepayments</li><li>Endowments</li><li>Restricted Gifts, Bequests, Donations</li><li>Cost-Sharing and Joint Project Agreements</li><li>Trust Accounts</li><li>Deposit Accounts</li><li>Court Awards</li></ul><p>As noted in the section 1.2 Limitations of the Manual, it is not possible to cover all transactions and Scenario s. This 
is particularly appropriate for some types of SPAs where within each type there is a wide range of possible situations. 
One or two Scenario s will be presented for each type of SPA listed below.</p><h4>References</h4><ul><li><em><a href="/pol/doc-eng.aspx?id=12249">Policy on Specified Purpose Accounts</a></em></li><li>PS 3100</li><li>Pages 4.10, 6.29 and 6.34 of Volume 1 of the 1999-2000 Public Accounts</li></ul><h4>9.1.1 Prepayments</h4><h4>Introduction</h4><p><strong>Authorities Perspective (Policy on Specified Purpose Accounts):</strong></p><p>When a department receives money from parties external to the Government in advance of goods or services being provided, 
the funds must be recorded as deferred revenue. However for government reporting purposes, the deferred revenue may either 
be credited to a regular deferred revenue account or a specified purpose account (SPA) depending on whether the goods or 
services to be provided are specified. Where the goods or services to be provided are specified, the money received is credited 
to a deferred revenue account and a non-tax revenue authority (see section 4.2 of the Manual for guidance). Where the goods 
or services to be provided are unspecified, the moneys received are also credited to a deferred revenue account (but specific 
to SPAs) and the authority credited is a SPA authority.</p><p>The distinction between specified and unspecified goods and services is important for spending authority. Where a department 
has the authority to re-spend revenues, the following differences exist:</p><ul><li>for specified goods and services, the amount received is re-spendable when cash is received;</li><li>for unspecified goods and services, the amount received is re-spendable only when the goods or services are provided. 
  Hence the authority to spend the revenue has been deferred until it is earned.</li></ul><p>Amounts equivalent to the cost of the goods or services will be transferred from the SPA to revenue as goods or services 
are provided, just as if payment had been made at the time, as per section 6(a) and (b) of the <em>Policy on Specified Purpose 
Accounts.</em></p><h4>References</h4><ul><li><em><a href="/pol/doc-eng.aspx?id=12249">Policy on Specified Purpose Accounts</a></em> - Appendix A Section 6</li><li>PSA 3100.11</li><li>CICA 4410.31</li></ul><h4>Scenario A</h4><p>Department enters in an agreement with a 3<sup>rd</sup> party to provide goods and services of an unspecified nature 
and amount. The 3<sup>rd</sup> party is required to make the payment of $10,000 in advance. The Department has the authority 
to respend revenue.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) Third Party gives Department $10,000 in advance of service being received.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Cash in Hands of Depts awaiting deposits to RG</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>10,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11125</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5299</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Deferred revenues - SPAs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>10,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23451</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N/P(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6081/6099</p></td></tr></table><div class="indent1"><p>(See section on Cash for the other cash related ledger entries)</p></div><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> Since cash for unspecified goods/services has been received but services are yet 
to be performed, a liability must be set up in the form of a deferred revenue account. The Department must indicate an increase 
in their cash holdings by debiting Cash in Hands of Depts. awaiting deposit to RG.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> When non-tax receipts for unspecified goods/services are received by the 
department prior to the Department providing the goods or services, the entire amount of the receipts should be recorded 
as an authority under "Other Specified Purpose Accounts". N/P(*), either a statutory on non statutory authority could be 
appropriate depending on the situation. Either of the following statutory authorities may be appropriate depending on the 
circumstances - N3xx or N5xx. If a non-statutory authority is required, any one of the following may be appropriate depending 
on the situation: P3xx, P5xx, P7xx or P8xx. Since, there is no impact on the authority side for cash, R300 should be used.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> To record the net impact on the SPA a department could use object "6081 -Deposit received" 
or object "6099-Net Increases or Decreases in Other SPAs" depending on whether detailed object information is desired. To 
record the net impact on cash accounts "5299 - Net Increase or Decrease in Cash Accounts should be used.</p><p>2) Goods/ services worth $5,000 are provided by the department and recognized as revenue</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Deferred Revenues - SPAs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,750</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23451</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N/P(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6086\6099</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Revenue</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4231X</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D/E(**)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4XXX</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR GST Payable</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>350</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21134</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR PST Payable</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>400</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21151</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><div class="indent1"><p>(Assumption: Sale takes place in Ontario. See section on Sale Tax for rules on sale tax with respect to sales in other 
  provinces.)</p><p>The entries for the settlement of GST payable can be found in the section related to Sales Tax Section.</p><p>See Accounts Payable Section for entries related to the settlement of PST Payable.</p></div><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> As good/services are provided, the liability "Deferred revenue - SPA" would be 
reduced and the equivalent amount would be credited to the appropriate revenue account (excluding the GST and PST). The 
GST and PST are charged directly to the SPA for the portion of expenditures incurred by the SPA, therefore $5,750 (1.15 
x $5,000) is recorded. The GST and PST would be accrued as a payable since the amount owing has not been paid.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> As goods/services are provided the liability account is charged for their 
costs. N/P(*), the same authority code used to set up the liability account would be used in this transaction. D/E(**) as 
the goods/services are provided the revenue should be charged to any one of the applicable codes depending on the situation, 
either D211 to D213 (if a statutory authority) or E211 to E213 (if a non-statutory authority). GST payable and PST payable 
do not affect authorities, therefore R300 is used.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> The object code to use for revenue depends on the goods or services being provided. 
To record the net impact on the SPA, object "6086 - Payments made in accordance with authorities" or "6099-Net Increases 
or Decreases in Other SPAs" could be used depending on whether detailed object information is desired. "6299- Net Increase 
or Decrease to Other Liability accounts" should be used to indicate the establishment of the GST payable and PST Payable 
and accounts payable.</p><p>See Scenario A Journal entry 2</p><p>3) Once the goods are provided the Department has authority to respend the revenue.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Revenue</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4231X</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>D218/E218</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4888</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Revenue</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4231X</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B13A</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4888</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> There is no affect on accruals here. This is strictly an authority transaction. 
To ensure that the FRAs are not affected the same FRA is debited and credited for the same amount.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> In order to indicate that the department can respend the revenue it receives, 
the revenue is credited to "B13A - Revenue credited to the vote". The debit side of the entry is coded to D218/E218 (depending 
whether the situation calls for statutory or non-statutory authority). It should be noted that these codes (D218/E218) have 
no affect on appropriations or authorities.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> There is no impact on objects. Therefore the same code for the same amount is used 
to indicate this. In this case "4888-Re-allocation from non-budgetary funds and accounts" is used.</p><h4>Departmental Financial Statement Presentation and Disclosure Requirements</h4><p>Amounts recorded in the Deferred revenue account - SPAs that are outstanding at year-end will be recorded under the heading 
Liabilities in the Department's Statement of Financial Position.</p><h4>9.1.2 Endowments</h4><h4>Introduction</h4><p><strong>Authorities Perspective (Policy on Specified Purpose Accounts):</strong></p><p>Endowments to the Crown are funds acquired by donation or bequest subject to the following conditions:</p><ol class="lower-alpha"><li>a formal agreement exists between the donor and the department responsible for the administration of the endowment 
  fund;</li><li>the agreement outlines the mechanisms governing the administration of the fund and the terms of interest payments;</li><li>the agreement specifies that only interest income may be spent for the specified purpose and that the capital must 
  be maintained intact.</li></ol><p><strong>Accrual Accounting Perspective:</strong></p><p>Endowment contributions will never be available to a department to use towards its expenses. Therefore the amount of 
the endowment should be recognized as an increase in net assets\net liabilities.</p><p>With respect to the interest income derived from the endowment, the portion of interest is earmarked for a specific purpose 
for future periods should be recorded as deferred revenue (liability) and recognized as revenue in the same period as related 
expenditures are made (see Scenario A). PS 3100.11.</p><h4>References</h4><ul><li>CICA 4410.29 and.49</li><li>PSA 3100.11</li><li><em><a href="/pol/doc-eng.aspx?id=12249">Policy on Specified Purpose Accounts</a></em> - Appendix A Section 4</li></ul><h4>Scenario A - Endowment is set up and all interest income is earmarked.</h4><p>J. Doe gives a Department an endowment of $500,000, specifying that all the interest earned is to be spent for the maintenance 
of a particular heritage building. This year the fund earned 5%.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) J Doe gives Department endowment of $500,000</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Cash in Hands of Depts awaiting deposits to RG</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>500,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11125</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5299</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Donations and bequests to endowment accounts</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>500,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>42624</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>L/M*</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8290</p></td></tr></table><div class="indent1"><p>(See section on Cash for the other cash related ledger entries)</p></div><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> The principal amount of the endowment is credited to a special category of revenue 
and the cash in the hands of the department is increased by an equivalent amount.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> L/M*, any endowment funds received by a Department are credited to the appropriate 
authority code specific to the endowment, either an "L" code for statutory accounts or an "M" code for non-statutory accounts.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> To record the net impact on Cash Accounts, 5299 would be used. To record the receipt 
of endowment funds "8290 - Other receipts" would be used.</p><p>2) End of year closing of FRA 42624</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Donations and bequests to endowment accounts</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>500,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>42624</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>XXXX*</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>XXXX*</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Endowment accounts</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>500,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>31224</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>XXXX*</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>XXXX*</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> At year-end, FRA 42624 is closed to a restricted net asset account FRA 31224.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> XXXX*, the authority codes depend on how each department's system closes 
and rolls-over. These codes do not roll-over for CFMRS purposes.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> XXXX*, the object codes depend on how each department's system closes and rolls-over. 
These codes do not roll-over for CFMRS purposes.</p><p>3) Endowment earns interest at a rate 5% per annum - entry must be done by inter-departmental entries and settled via 
inter-departmental settlement (IS) entries.</p><div class="indent1"><p>3a) Creditor side entry by department.</p></div><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Other receivables from O.G.D.s</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11242</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5399</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Deferred Revenue - SPAs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23451</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N6/P4*</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6099/6082</p></td></tr></table><div class="indent1"><p>3a) Debtor side entry by Department of Finance.</p></div><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Interest on other non-budgetary accounts</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>52242</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>A701</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3114</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Other payables to O.G.D.s</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21132</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> Interest earned of $25,000 (5% x $500,000) on the endowment is a public debt charge 
(interest expense). Earnings from the endowment go into a deferred revenue account. However, as the authority for the interest 
on public debt is under the Department of Finance, the entries must be recorded as O.G.D. receivables\payables until they 
are settled via the IS process.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> As interest is earned on the endowment, it will be charged against "A701-Interest 
on unmatured debt" by the Department of Finance. The earnings of the endowment will be credited to the specific authority 
code established for the interest portion of the endowment. For statutory accounts, the code is in the N61x range and for 
non-statutory accounts the code is in the P41x range. The authority code is different than the code used to record the endowment 
principal due to the different accounting treatment required for the principal and interest portions of the endowment. As 
the IS receivable and payable do not affect authorities, "R300 - Total amounts of all other assets and of all other liabilities" 
is used.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> "3114 - Interest on SPAs/Interest on Other Liabilities" is used to reflect the interest 
charge on the endowment fund. "6099-Net Increases or Decreases in Other SPAs" or "6082 - Interest received" would be used 
to reflect interest earned on the endowment. "5399 - Net increase or decrease in accounts receivable" and "6299 -Net increase 
or decrease in other liability" would be used for the IS accounts.</p><p>4a) Interest earned on the endowment is spent for specified purpose as per the agreement.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Operating Expenses</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N6/P4*</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>04xx</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accounts Payable</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> The expenses are charged to the operating expenses FRA.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> The expense is charged to the authority code that was used to record the 
interest on the endowment account. There is no impact on authorities for the accounts payable so the code to be used would 
be "R300 - All other assets and liabilities".</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> The appropriate object code would be used depending on the nature of the expenses. 
"6299 -Net increase or decrease in other liability" would be used for the accounts payable.</p><p>4b) The equivalent amount of expenses are drawn down and recognized as revenue.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Deferred Revenue - SPAs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23451</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F450</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6099/6089</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Interest on endowments</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>25,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>42724</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F259</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4888</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> Externally restricted inflows are recognized as revenue in the period in which 
the resources are used for the purpose or purposes specified. Since $25,000 of interest on the endowment fund has been used, 
this amount is recorded as revenue. The charges to deferred revenue are equivalent to the amount of expenses incurred to 
satisfy the specified purpose.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> This is strictly an accrual transaction. There is no impact on authorities/appropriations 
since the authority was charged when the operating expenses were recorded.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> "6099 - Net Increases or Decreases in Other SPAs" or "6089 -Other adjustments" would 
be used on the debit side of the transaction. "4888 Reallocation from non-budgetary funds and accounts" would be used to 
reflect the reallocation of the deferred revenue to revenue.</p><h4>Departmental Financial Statement Presentation and Disclosure Requirements</h4><p>Endowments will be disclosed on the Department's Statement of Financial Position under the heading Net Assets (Liabilities) 
as a restricted asset. The nature, amounts and terms of the endowments should be disclosed in the notes to the financial 
statements. Interest earned but not yet spent for a specified purpose will be recorded as deferred revenue and reported 
under the heading Liabilities in the Department's Statement of Financial Position.</p><h4>9.1.3 Restricted Gifts, Bequests, Donations</h4><h4>Introduction</h4><p><strong>Authorities Perspective: Policy on Specified Purpose Accounts</strong></p><p>Gifts, bequests and donations to the Crown may be made with or without conditions.</p><ol class="lower-alpha"><li>Any amounts received for <strong>a specified purpose</strong>, <strong>as unconditional or general</strong> gifts, 
  bequests or donations must be spent in accordance with mandate of the organization.</li></ol><p>Any amounts received as <strong>conditional contributions where object of expenditure is clear</strong><strong>and specific</strong> 
are to be used only for the stated purpose. If the amount cannot be spent for specific purpose, the money is to be returned 
to the donor.</p><p><strong>Accrual Accounting Perspective:</strong></p><p>Donations are treated differently depending on whether they are restricted donations or unrestricted donations.</p><p><strong>Restricted Contributions:</strong></p><p>If the external parties specify how the resources are to be used, those inflows are restricted in nature. For example, 
a third party donates money conditional on it being spent on medical research. This would constitute an external restriction 
since the asset is restricted by agreement with the external party.</p><p>Restricted contributions for the purchase of capital assets that will be amortized should be deferred and recognized 
as revenue on the same basis as the amortization expense relate to the acquired capital assets (CICA 4410.33). However, 
if the contribution does not specify that the funds are to be spent on a capital asset, then the contribution would be recognized 
as revenue when spent regardless of the fact that some of the expenditures may relate to the purchase of a capital asset.</p><p>Contributions used for the purpose of purchasing capital assets that fall below the Department's capital asset threshold 
would be reported as a liability and recognized as revenue in the period in which the expense is recognized. This is construed 
to be using the resources used for the purpose specified (PS 3100.11).</p><p><strong>Unrestricted Contributions:</strong></p><p>Unrestricted contributions (i.e. cash) should be recognized as revenue in the current period (CICA 4410.47). See Section 
6.2 - Unrestricted Gifts, Donation and Bequests for guidance on accounting for unrestricted contributions.</p><h4>References</h4><ul><li><em><a href="/pol/doc-eng.aspx?id=12249">Policy on Specified Purpose Accounts</a></em> - Appendix A 
  Section 4</li><li>CICA 4410, 4430</li><li>PS 3100</li></ul><h4>Scenario A - Donation for specified purpose (unconditional or conditional)</h4><p>An individual gives a department $200,000 to be spent on scientific research (specified purpose) which is in line with 
the Department's mandate.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>To record donation of $200,000</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Cash in Hands of Depts awaiting deposits to RG</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>200,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11125</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5299</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Deferred Revenue -SPAs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>200,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23451</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N6/P4*</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6099/6081</p></td></tr></table><div class="indent1"><p>(See section on Cash for the other cash related ledger entries)</p></div><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> Since cash has been received but the specified purpose has not been carried out, 
the donation must be credited to deferred revenues. The Department must indicate an increase in their cash holdings by debiting 
Cash in the Hands of Depts awaiting deposits to RG.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> N6/P4*, the donation will be credited to the authority code established 
for the specific SPA. For statutory accounts, the authority code is in the N6xx range and for non-statutory accounts the 
authority code is in the P4xx range. Since there is no impact on the authority side for cash, R300 should be used.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> To record the net impact on Cash Accounts, 5299 would be used. To record the net impact 
on the SPA "6099-Net Increases or Decreases in Other SPAs" or "6081 - Deposits received" would be used.</p><p>2) To record costs incurred for specified purpose - assume $50,000 spent.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Operating expenses</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>50,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N6/P4</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>0430</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR GST Refundable Advance Account</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3,500</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>13392</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>G111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8171</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accounts Payable</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>53,500</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><div class="indent1"><p>See the Accounts Payable section of the manual to see related entries required for the settlement of the accounts payable. 
  See the GST/HST section of the manual to see related entries required for the settlement of the GST.</p></div><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> The expenses are charged to operating expenses FRA.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> The expense is charged to the original authority which was used to record 
the SPA in entry 1. Since GST is not to be charged to a departmental appropriation, it is set up as an advance under a special 
authority, G111. There is no impact on authorities for the accounts payable so the code to be used would be "R300-All other 
assets and liabilities"</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> "0430 - Scientific services, excluding consultants" is used as scientific research 
was the specified purpose of the donation. "8171 - Payment of GST on purchases" would be used for the GST component. "6299 
- Net increase or decrease in other liability" would be used for accounts payable.</p><p>3) To recognize revenue from SPA and draw down deferred revenue.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Deferred Revenue - SPAs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>50,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23451</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F450</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6099/6089</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Donations and bequests</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>50,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>42725</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F259</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4888</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> Externally restricted inflows are recognized as revenue in the period in which 
the resources are used for the purpose or purposes specified. Since $50,000 of the donation has been used, this amount is 
recorded as revenue. The charges to deferred revenue are equivalent to the amount of expenses incurred to satisfy the specified 
purpose.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> This is strictly an accrual transaction. There is no impact on authorities/appropriations 
since the authority was charged when the operating expenses were recorded.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> To record the net impact on the SPA "6099-Net Increases or Decreases in Other SPAs" 
or "6089 - Other adjustments" would be used. " To reflect incoming revenue in the period "4888-Re-allocation from non-budgetary 
funds and accounts" would be used.</p><h4>Scenario B - Restricted Contribution for purchase of tangible capital asset greater than Departmental capital 
asset threshold (assume threshold is $10,000).</h4><p>In year 1, a third party gives a department $21,000 and specifies that it is to be used for the purchase of a truck. 
The vehicle is not purchased until year 2 and has a useful life of 7 years with no residual value.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) To record the receipt of the cash ($21,000) in year 1.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Cash in the hands of the Depts awaiting deposit to RG</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11125</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5299</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Deferred Revenue -SPAs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23451</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N6/P4*</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6099/6081</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> Since the money donated is to be used for a specified purpose, this qualifies 
as a restricted contribution. Since the requirement to buy a truck has not been met, the cash received must be recorded 
as deferred revenue. The Department must indicate an increase in their cash holdings by debiting "Cash in the Hands of Depts 
awaiting deposits to RG".</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> Same as entry 1 in Scenario B.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> Same as entry 1 in Scenario B.</p><p>2) To record the purchase of the truck in year 2.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Vehicle</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16133</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N6/P4</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1261</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR GST Refundable Advance</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1,470</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>13392</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>G111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8171</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accounts Payable</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>22,470</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><div class="indent1"><p>(See Accounts Payable section for entries related to the settlement of Accounts Payable)<br></br>
  (See Sales Tax section for entries related to the settlement of GST)</p></div><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> The department must capitalize the acquisition of the vehicle on their books since 
it exceeds the capital asset threshold of $10,000. At this point the Department is being charged GST on the vehicle, and 
must pay it to the vendor. However, as the Department will eventually recover this amount from Canada Customs and Revenue 
Agency (CCRA) it should be recorded as an asset in "13392 GST/HST Refundable advance accounts". The associated amount owed 
of $22,470 but not yet paid must be recorded in the form of a payable.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> At this point the vehicle is being purchased with money that is held in 
the SPA. Therefore, the authority code used to record the SPA is charged the cost of the vehicle. Since GST is not to be 
charged to a departmental appropriation, it is set up as an advance under a special authority, G111. Since accounts payable 
does not affect appropriations, the R300 authority code is used.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> The acquisition of a vehicle will affect the economic objects at this point. 
In this case 1261 is used in this example since the purchase was motor vehicle. "6299- Net Increase or Decrease to Other 
Liability accounts" is used to establish the amount owing. The GST must be reflected by using, "8171-Payment of GST on purchases".</p><p>3) Periodic amortization expense for the capital asset</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Amortization expense</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51433</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3451</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accumulated amortization-Mach. &amp; Equip.</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16233</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F311</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>7061/7099</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> The yearly amortization expense of $3,000 is calculated as follows ($21,000/7years). 
See Section on Tangible Capital Assets for additional coding rationale.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> See Section on Tangible Capital Assets for coding rationale.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> See Section on Tangible Capital Assets for coding rationale.</p><p>4) Periodic adjustment to move the equivalent of the resources consumed (amortization) from the Deferred Revenue account</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Deferred Revenue - SPAs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23451</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F450</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6099/6089</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Donations and bequests</p></th><td class="alignTopRight">
</td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>3,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>42725</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F259</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> Restricted contributions for the purchase of capital assets that will be amortized 
should be deferred and recognized as revenue on the same basis as the amortization expense related to the acquired capital 
assets, therefore $3,000 is brought into revenue.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> This is strictly an accrual transaction. There is no impact on authorities/appropriations 
since the authority was charged when the truck was purchased.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> To record the net impact on the SPA "6099-Net Increases or Decreases in Other 
SPAs" or "6089- Other adjustments" would be used. " To reflect incoming revenue in the period "4888-Re-allocation from non-budgetary 
funds and accounts" would be used.</p><p><strong>Note:</strong> If the donation only specified that the funds were to be used towards some endeavour (e.g. agricultural 
research) and the department used the funds to purchase an asset, the revenue would be recognized entirely in the year the 
asset was purchased. Under GAAP, the deferral and recognition of revenue over the life of the asset is only required when 
the donor specifies that a capital asset is to be purchased with the funds.</p><h4>Scenario C - Restricted Contribution for the purchase of land</h4><p>A third party donates $11,000 to a Department. The individual specifies that the money be used for the purchase of land.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) To record the receipt of $11,000.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Cash in Hands of Depts awaiting deposit to RG</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11125</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5299</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Deferred Revenue - SPAs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23451</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N6/P4*</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6099/6081</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> Since the money donated us to be used for a specified purpose that has not yet 
been performed, the cash received must be recorded as a deferred revenue.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> same as entry #1 in Scenario B.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> same as entry #1 in Scenario B.</p><p>2) Once the land is purchased the contribution is no longer restricted.</p><div class="indent1"><p>2a) Record the purchase of land.</p></div><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Land</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>16111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N6/P4</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1301</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accounts Payable</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> The purchase of land is recorded as an asset and the corresponding amount is set 
up as a payable for the amount owing.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> Authorities are charged when there is an acquisition of goods and services. 
The authority code used to record the donation (N6xx or P4xx) is charged directly for the purchase of the land. Since accounts 
payable does not affect appropriations, R300 is used.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> At this point land has been acquired, therefore 1301 would be used. "6299- 
Net Increase or Decrease to Other Liability accounts" should be used to indicate the establishment of the accounts payable.</p><div class="indent1"><p>2b) Condition of contribution is satisfied therefore liability is reduced and revenue is recorded.</p></div><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Deferred revenue - SPAs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23451</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F450</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6099/6089</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Donations and bequests</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>42725</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F259</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4888</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> Once the land is purchased the contribution is no longer considered restricted. 
Therefore, the liability is reduced and there is a corresponding increase to the revenue account.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> There is no impact on authorities/appropriations since the authority was 
charged when the land was purchased. F codes will be used in order to assist in departmental reconciliations. "F450- Other 
non-appropriated amounts added to or deducted from liability balances" would be used for the deferred revenue amount. "F259- 
Other revenue not being credited to appropriations or other authorities at the same time" should be used for the revenue 
amount.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> To record the net impact on the SPA "6099-Net Increases or Decreases in Other 
SPAs" or "6089 - Other adjustments" would be used. " To reflect incoming revenue in the period "4888-Re-allocation from 
non-budgetary funds and accounts" would be used.</p><h4>Scenario D - Contribution is for purchase of an asset less than departmental capital asset threshold. (assume 
departmental threshold is $10,000).</h4><p>A third party donates $5,000 to a Department. The individual specifies that the money be used for the purchase of research 
equipment.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) To record the receipt of the cash ($5,000) in year 1.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Cash in the hands of the Depts awaiting deposit to RG</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11125</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5299</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Deferred Revenue - SPAs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23451</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N6/P4*</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6099/6081</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> Since the requirement to buy the research equipment has not been met, the cash 
received must be recorded as deferred revenue. The Department must indicate an increase in their cash holdings by debiting 
Cash in the Hands of Depts awaiting deposits to RG.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> same as entry #1 in Scenario B.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> same as entry #1 in Scenario B.</p><p>2) To record the purchase of the research equipment and recognize revenue as resources are used for the purpose specified.</p><div class="indent1"><p>2a) To record the purchase of the research equipment in year 2.</p></div><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Operating Expense</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N6/P4</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>1261</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR GST Refundable Advance</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>350</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>13392</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>G111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8171</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accounts Payable</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,350</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><div class="indent1"><p>(See Accounts Payable section for entries related to the settlement of Accounts Payable)<br></br>
  (See Sales Tax section for entries related to the settlement of GST)</p></div><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> Since the amount of the purchase is less than the department's capital asset threshold, 
the cost of the equipment will be charged to an operating expense. At this point the Department is being charged GST on 
the research equipment, and must pay it to the vendor. However, as the Department will eventually recover this amount from 

Canada Customs and Revenue Agency (CCRA) it should be recorded as an asset in "13392 GST/HST Refundable advance accounts". 
The associated amount owed of $5,350 but not yet paid must be recorded in the form of a payable.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> Since accounts payable does not affect appropriations, the R300 authority 
code is used. At this point the research equipment is being purchased with money that is held in the deposit account. Therefore, 
the authority used to record the donation is charged the cost of the research equipment. Since GST is not to be charged 
to a departmental appropriation, it is set up as an advance under a special authority, G111.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> The acquisition of research equipment will affect the economic objects at this 
point. In this case 1261 is used in this example since the purchase was research equipment. "6299- Net Increase or Decrease 
to Other Liability accounts" is used to establish the amount owing. Since GST/HST is payable to the, the GST must be reflected 
by using, "8171-Payment of GST on purchases".</p><div class="indent1"><p>2b) To move the equivalent of the resources consumed from the Deferred Revenue account into revenue</p></div><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Deferred Revenue - SPAs</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23451</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F450</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6099/6089</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Donations and bequests</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>42725</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>F259</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4888</p></td></tr></table><p><strong>FRA coding rationale:</strong> Contributions used for the purpose of purchasing capital assets that fall below 
the Department's capital asset threshold would be reported as a liability and recognized as revenue in the period in which 
the expenses are incurred for the purpose specified. Therefore $5,000 is brought into revenue.</p><p><strong>Authority coding rationale:</strong> This is strictly an accrual transaction. There is no impact on authorities/appropriations 
since the authority was charged when the equipment was purchased. F codes will be used in order to assist in departmental 
reconciliations. "F450- Other non-appropriated amounts added to or deducted from liability balances" would be used for the 
deferred revenue amount. "F259- Other revenue not being credited to appropriations or other authorities at the same time" 
should be used for the revenue amount.</p><p><strong>Object coding rationale:</strong> To record the net impact on the SPA "6099-Net Increases or Decreases in Other 
SPAs" or "6089- Other adjustments" would be used. To reflect incoming revenue in the period "4888-Re-allocation from non-budgetary 
funds and accounts" would be used.</p><h4>Departmental Financial Statement Presentation and Disclosure Requirements</h4><p>Restricted gifts, bequests and donations not yet spent for a specified purpose will be recorded as deferred revenue and 
reported under the heading Liabilities in the Department's Statement of Financial Position.</p><p>Financial statements should disclose in the notes or schedules:</p><ol class="lower-alpha"><li>a general description of the nature and source of any external restrictions;</li><li>the amounts of externally restricted inflows by major source; and</li><li>the amounts of, and changes in, the deferred revenue balance attributable to each major category of external restrictions;</li></ol><h4>9.1.4 Cost-Sharing and Joint Project Agreements</h4><h4>Introduction</h4><p><strong>Authorities Perspective: Policy on Specified Purpose Accounts</strong></p><p>Cost-sharing agreements are arrangements whereby the parties involved agree to share specified costs but not to participate 
directly in or assign staff to a common undertaking.</p><p>Joint project agreements are arrangements whereby the parties involved agree to participate jointly in the actual carrying 
out of a project. This would involve the sharing of resources, the purchase of goods and services, the hiring of personnel, 
and so on.</p><p>A specified purpose account is required under a cost-sharing or joint project agreement <strong>only</strong> when funds 
are received in advance from the external parties to the agreement. Funds received from outside parties for the purposes 
of cost-sharing or joint project agreements must never be used to reimburse departmental expenditures; expenditures shall 
be charged directly to the account.</p><p>It is the responsibility of departments to ensure that their use of specified purpose accounts complies with the Policy 
on Specified Purpose Accounts.</p><p><strong>Accrual Accounting Perspective:</strong></p><p>There are two alternatives for accounting for the funds advanced under a cost-sharing or joint project agreement. The 
accounting treatment selected depends upon whether the funds received from the outside party are an advance to cover future 
expenses that belong to the outside party or are a contribution towards expenses to be incurred by the department.</p><p>Where the funds received are considered an advance to cover the outside party's future expenses, the specified purpose 
account would represent a liability of the department. Any expenses funded from the SPA would not be recorded in the accounts 
of Canada but would simply represent a reduction in the SPA. No revenues would be recorded in this Scenario. See Scenario 
A for the accounting entries. An example of this Scenario is where a department arranges missions overseas and invites third 
parties to participate but they must pay their own travel expenses. The third party advances funds to the department to 
pay the expenses on its behalf. It would be inappropriate for the department to recognize these funds as revenue and expenses 
as it has simply acted as a facilitator in this case.</p><p>Where the funds received are considered a contribution towards expenses to be incurred by the department, the funds would 
be recorded as deferred revenue. Expenses would be recorded in the accounts of Canada (but under the authority of the SPA) 
and revenue would be recorded to reduce the balance of the deferred revenue account. Scenario B presents an example of this 
type of agreement.</p><p>Departments should review the cost-sharing and joint project agreements to determine which accounting treatment best 
reflects the substance of the arrangement with the external party. In addition to the above, departments should consider 
the appropriateness of excluding or including the activities funded by these agreements from their financial statements. 
Under Scenario A, the receipts and disbursements related to the SPA accounts will not be recorded as revenues and expenses 
in the income statement. If SPA funds are used to pay for a significant amount of employee salaries or other internal costs, 
excluding these expenses reduces the usefulness of the income statement in conveying of the department's activities in the 
year.</p><h4>References</h4><ul><li><em><a href="/pol/doc-eng.aspx?id=12249">Policy on Specified Purpose Accounts</a></em> - Appendix B 
  Section 2.2</li><li>PS1500.39</li></ul><h4>Scenario A</h4><p>A Department enters into a cost sharing agreement 60/40 - (60% of costs to be charged to the Department and 40% to the 
outside party) with an outside party. The agreement calls for the outside party to advance the Department $100,000 to cover 
its share of expenses to be incurred under a scientific research project. The funds will cover the costs of hiring an external 
consultant and purchasing research equipment. This money is deposited in a SPA.</p><p>Consulting fees of $10,000 are incurred. The equipment purchased, cost $40,000 in total and has a useful life of 5 years 
and will have no residual value. The agreement specifies that the asset is to remain the property of the department at the 
end of the project.</p><h4>Journal Entries</h4><p>1) A private-sector company gives the Department $100,000 as their contribution to a cost sharing agreement.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Cash in Hands of Depts awaiting deposits to RG</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>100,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>11125</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>5299</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Other SPA accounts (liability)</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>100,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23441</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N/P(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6081/6099</p></td></tr></table><div class="indent1"><p>(See section on Cash for the cash related ledger entries)</p></div><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> Since cash has been received but services are yet to be performed, a liability 
must be set up under "Other Specified Purpose Accounts". The Department must indicate an increase in their cash holdings 
by debiting "Cash in Hands of Depts. awaiting deposit to RG".</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> The funds received should be recorded as an authority under "Other Specified 
Purpose Accounts". N/P(*) either a statutory or non-statutory authority could be appropriate depending on the situation. 
Any one of the following statutory authorities may be used - N3xx or N5xx, or, if a non-statutory authority is required, 
any one of the following would be appropriate depending on the situation - P3xx, P5xx, P7xx or P8xx. Since there is no impact 
on the authority side for cash, R300 is used.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> To record the net impact on the SPA a department could use object "6081 -Deposit received" 
or object "6099-Net Increases or Decreases in Other SPAs" depending on whether detailed object information is desired. To 
record the net impact on cash accounts "5299 - Net Increase or Decrease in Cash Accounts should be used.</p><p>2) As part of the cost-sharing agreement, the Department shares 60/40 with the outside party in all expenses incurred 
for the research project. $10,000 in consulting fees are incurred and the SPA is drawn down.</p><div class="indent1"><p>2a) $10,000 in consulting fees are incurred.</p></div><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Operating expenses</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6,000</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>51321</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>B11A(**)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>04xx</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Other SPA accounts (liability)</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>4,280</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>23441</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>N/P(*)</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6086/6099</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR GST/HST Refundable advance account</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>420</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>13392</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>G111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>8171</p></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>CR Accounts payable</p></th><td class="alignTopRight"><p>10,700</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>21111</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>R300</p></td><td class="alignTopRight"><p>6299</p></td></tr></table><div class="indent1"><p>See Accounts Payable section for journal entries regarding settlement of accounts payable.</p><p>See Sales Tax section for journal entries regarding the settlement of the GST/HST Refundable advance accounts.</p><p><strong>Note:</strong> whether or not GST is charged to the SPA account will depend upon the terms of the agreement 
  with the outside party. If GST is not to be charged, the SPA account would only be charged $4,000 while the GST refundable 
  advance account would be charged $700.</p></div><p><strong>FRA Coding Rationale:</strong> Since the expense was incurred as part of a cost-sharing agreement, the Department 
would only record its share of the expense (60% of $10,000). The remaining share of the expense (40%) plus applicable taxes 
would be charged directly to the SPA liability account. The department would only charge its share of the GST to the refundable 
advance account as the outside party would pay its own taxes. The cost of the operating expenses plus 7% GST ($10,000+700) 
would be accrued as an accounts payable in the period since expenses were incurred but not yet paid.</p><p><strong>Authority Coding Rationale:</strong> Authorities are charged when there is an acquisition of goods or services. 
Since consulting services have been acquired, an appropriation or other source of funding must be charged. Only $6,000 should 
be charged to the Departmental appropriation. B11A(**), in this example, the departmental portion of the acquisition of 
consulting services would be charged to either a B11A - Program Vote, or B12A Operating Vote.The $4,000 operating expenses 
not being funded from departmental appropriations is charged to the SPA. N/P(*), any one of the following statutory authorities 
can be used depending on the situation - N3xx or N5xx,or, if a non-statutory authority is required, any one of the following 
can be used depending on the situation: P3xx, P5xx, P7xx or P8xx). Since GST is not to be charged to a departmental appropriation, 
authority G111 is used. Accounts payable does not impact appropriation, therefore, R300 is used.</p><p><strong>Object Rationale:</strong> Since the consulting services were acquired at this point, the appropriate object 
must be used which in this case would be 04xx. "6086 - Payments made in accordance with authorities" or "6099 - Increases 
or decreases in other SPA" could be used for the expense charged to the SPA depending on whether detailed object information 
is desired. Since there has been an acquisition of services on which GST/HST is payable, the related GST must be reflected 
by using, "8171-Payment of GST on purchases". "6299- Net Increase or Decrease to Other Liability accounts" should be used 
to indicate the establishment of accounts payable.</p><p><strong>Alternate entries:</strong> If a department's system cannot accommodate the above entry, an alternate entry which 
charges 100% of the expense to the Government with a subsequent reallocation to the SPA can also be performed.</p><p>First entry:</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AMT($)</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>FRA</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>AUTH</strong></p></th><th scope="col" class="alignTopRight"><p><strong>OBJ</strong></p></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="alignTop"><p>DR Operating $40,000 is paid for an item considered a capital asset.</p><table class="table table-bordered table-condensed"><tr><th scope="col" class="alignTop"> </th><th scope="col"
